    43	  private Token nextString() {
    44	    var scope = interpolationStack.getFirst();
    45	    if (stringEnded) {
    46	      lexStringEnd(scope);
    47	      stringEnded = false;
    48	      interpolationStack.pop();
    49	      state = State.DEFAULT;
    50	      return Token.STRING_END;
    51	    }
    52	    if (lookahead == EOF) return Token.EOF;
    53	    if (isEscape) {
    54	      isEscape = false;
    55	      // consume the `\#*`
    56	      for (var i = 0; i < scope.pounds + 1; i++) {
    57	        nextChar();
    58	      }
    59	      return lexEscape();
    60	    }
    61	    if (scope.quotes == 1) {
    62	      lexString(scope.pounds);
    63	    } else {
    64	      if (lookahead == '\r') {
    65	        nextChar();
    66	        if (lookahead == '\n') {
    67	          nextChar();
    68	        }
    69	        return Token.STRING_NEWLINE;
    70	      }
    71	      if (lookahead == '\n') {
    72	        nextChar();
    73	        return Token.STRING_NEWLINE;
    74	      }
    75	      lexMultiString(scope.pounds);
    76	    }
    77	    return Token.STRING_PART;
    78	  }

    80	  private Token lexStringStartPounds() {
    81	    int pounds = 1;
    82	    while (lookahead == '#') {
    83	      nextChar();
    84	      pounds++;
    85	    }
    86	    if (lookahead == EOF) {
    87	      throw lexError(ErrorMessages.create("unexpectedEndOfFile"), span());
    88	    }
    89	    if (lookahead != '"') {
    90	      throw unexpectedChar(lookahead, "\"");
    91	    }
    92	    nextChar();
    93	    return lexStringStart(pounds);
    94	  }

    96	  private Token lexStringStart(int pounds) {
    97	    var quotes = 1;

    99	      nextChar();
   100	      if (lookahead == '"') {
   101	        nextChar();
   102	        quotes = 3;

   104	        backup();
   105	      }
   106	    }
   107	    state = State.STRING;
   108	    interpolationStack.push(new InterpolationScope(quotes, pounds));
   109	    stringEnded = false;
   110	    if (quotes == 1) return Token.STRING_START;
   111	    return Token.STRING_MULTI_START;
   112	  }

   114	  private void lexStringEnd(InterpolationScope scope) {

   121	  private void lexString(int pounds) {
   122	    var poundsInARow = 0;
   123	    var foundQuote = false;
   124	    var foundBackslash = false;
   125	    while (lookahead != EOF) {
   126	      var ch = nextChar();
   127	      switch (ch) {
   128	        case '\n', '\r' ->
   129	            throw lexError(
   130	                ErrorMessages.create("missingDelimiter", "\"" + "#".repeat(pounds)), cursor - 1, 1);
   131	        case '"' -> {
   132	          if (pounds == 0) {
   133	            backup();
   134	            stringEnded = true;
   135	            return;
   136	          }
   137	          foundQuote = true;
   138	          foundBackslash = false;
   139	          poundsInARow = 0;
   140	        }
   141	        case '\\' -> {
   142	          foundQuote = false;
   143	          foundBackslash = true;
   144	          poundsInARow = 0;
   145	          if (pounds == poundsInARow) {
   146	            backup(pounds + 1);
   147	            isEscape = true;
   148	            return;
   149	          }
   150	        }
   151	        case '#' -> {
   152	          poundsInARow++;
   153	          if (foundQuote && (pounds == poundsInARow)) {
   154	            backup(pounds + 1);
   155	            stringEnded = true;
   156	            return;
   157	          }
   158	          if (foundBackslash && pounds == poundsInARow) {
   159	            backup(pounds + 1);
   160	            isEscape = true;
   161	            return;
   162	          }
   163	        }
   164	        default -> {
   165	          foundQuote = false;
   166	          foundBackslash = false;
   167	          poundsInARow = 0;
   168	        }
   169	      }
   170	    }
   171	  }

     6	  private void lexExponent() {
     7	    if (lookahead == '+' || lookahead == '-') {
     8	      nextChar();
     9	    }
    10	    if (lookahead == '_') {
    11	      throw lexError("invalidSeparatorPosition");
    12	    }
    13	    if (lookahead < 48 || lookahead > 57) {
    14	      throw unexpectedChar(lookahead, "number");
    15	    }
    16	    while ((lookahead >= 48 && lookahead <= 57) || lookahead == '_') {
    17	      nextChar();
    18	    }
    19	  }
    20	
    21	  private void lexDotNumber() {
    22	    if (lookahead == '_') {
    23	      throw lexError("invalidSeparatorPosition");
    24	    }
    25	    while ((lookahead >= 48 && lookahead <= 57) || lookahead == '_') {
    26	      nextChar();
    27	    }
    28	    if (lookahead == 'e' || lookahead == 'E') {
    29	      nextChar();
    30	      lexExponent();
    31	    }
    32	  }
    33	
    34	  private Token lexShebang() {
    35	    do {
    36	      nextChar();
    37	    } while (lookahead != '\n' && lookahead != '\r' && lookahead != EOF);
    38	    return Token.SHEBANG;
    39	  }

    41	  private boolean isHex(char ch) {
    42	    var code = (int) ch;
    43	    return (code >= 48 && code <= 57) || (code >= 97 && code <= 102) || (code >= 65 && code <= 70);
    44	  }

    46	  private static boolean isIdentifierStart(char c) {
    47	    return c == '_' || c == '$' || Character.isUnicodeIdentifierStart(c);
    48	  }

    50	  private static boolean isIdentifierPart(char c) {
    51	    return c != EOF && (c == '$' || Character.isUnicodeIdentifierPart(c));
    52	  }

    54	  private char nextChar() {
    55	    var tmp = lookahead;
    56	    cursor++;
    57	    if (cursor >= size) {
    58	      lookahead = EOF;
    59	    } else {
    60	      lookahead = source[cursor];
    61	    }
    62	    return tmp;
    63	  }
    64	
    65	  private void backup() {
    66	    lookahead = source[--cursor];
    67	  }
    68	
    69	  private void backup(int amount) {
    70	    cursor -= amount;
    71	    lookahead = source[cursor];
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  private ParserError lexError(String msg, Object... args) {
    75	    var length = lookahead == EOF ? 0 : 1;
    76	    var index = lookahead == EOF ? cursor - 1 : cursor;
    77	    return new ParserError(ErrorMessages.create(msg, args), new Span(index, length));
    78	  }
    79	
    80	  private ParserError lexError(String msg, int charIndex, int length) {
    81	    return new ParserError(msg, new Span(charIndex, length));
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  private ParserError lexError(String msg, Span span) {
    85	    return new ParserError(msg, span);
    86	  }

    88	  private ParserError unexpectedChar(char got, String didYouMean) {
    89	    return lexError("unexpectedCharacter", got, didYouMean);
    90	  }

    92	  private ParserError unexpectedChar(String got, String option1, String option2, String option3) {
    93	    return lexError("unexpectedCharacter3", got, option1, option2, option3);
    94	  }

    90	@SuppressWarnings("DuplicatedCode")
    91	public class Parser {
    92	
    93	  private Lexer lexer;
    94	  private Token lookahead;
    95	  private Span spanLookahead;
    96	  private boolean backtracking = false;
    97	  private FullToken prev;
    98	  private FullToken _lookahead;
    99	  private boolean precededBySemicolon = false;
   100	
   101	  public Parser() {}
   102	
   103	  private void init(String source) {
   104	    this.lexer = new Lexer(source);
   105	    _lookahead = forceNext();
   106	    lookahead = _lookahead.token;
   107	    spanLookahead = _lookahead.span;
   108	  }
   109	
   110	  public Module parseModule(String source) {
   111	    init(source);
   112	    if (lookahead == Token.EOF) {
   113	      return new Module(Collections.singletonList(null), new Span(0, 0));
   114	    }
   115	    var start = spanLookahead;
   116	    Span end = null;
   117	    ModuleDecl moduleDecl;
   118	    var nodes = new ArrayList<Node>();
   119	    try {
   120	      var header = parseMemberHeader();
   121	
   122	      moduleDecl = parseModuleDecl(header);
   123	      if (moduleDecl != null) {
   124	        end = moduleDecl.span();
   125	        header = null;
   126	      }
   127	      nodes.add(moduleDecl);
   128	      // imports
   129	      while (lookahead == Token.IMPORT || lookahead == Token.IMPORT_STAR) {
   130	        if (header != null && header.isNotEmpty()) {
   131	          throw parserError("wrongHeaders", "Imports");
   132	        }
   133	        var _import = parseImportDecl();
   134	        nodes.add(_import);
   135	        end = _import.span();
   136	      }
   137	
   138	      // entries
   139	      if (header != null && header.isNotEmpty()) {
   140	        end = parseModuleMember(header, nodes);
   141	      }
   142	
   143	      while (lookahead != Token.EOF) {
   144	        header = parseMemberHeader();
   145	        end = parseModuleMember(header, nodes);
   146	      }
   147	      return new Module(nodes, start.endWith(spanLookahead));
   148	    } catch (ParserError pe) {
   149	      var spanEnd = end != null ? end : start;
   150	      pe.setPartialParseResult(new Module(nodes, start.endWith(spanEnd)));
   151	      throw pe;
   152	    }
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  public Expr parseExpressionInput(String source) {
   156	    init(source);
   157	    var expr = parseExpr();
   158	    expect(Token.EOF, "unexpectedToken", "end of file");
   159	    return expr;
   160	  }
   161	
   162	  public ReplInput parseReplInput(String source) {
   163	    init(source);
   164	    var nodes = new ArrayList<Node>();
   165	    while (lookahead != Token.EOF) {
   166	      var header = parseMemberHeader();
   167	      switch (lookahead) {
   168	        case IMPORT, IMPORT_STAR -> {
   169	          ensureEmptyHeaders(header, "Imports");
   170	          nodes.add(parseImportDecl());
   171	        }
   172	        case MODULE, AMENDS, EXTENDS -> nodes.add(parseModuleDecl(header));
   173	        case CLASS -> nodes.add(parseClass(header));
   174	        case TYPE_ALIAS -> nodes.add(parseTypeAlias(header));
   175	        case FUNCTION -> nodes.add(parseClassMethod(header));
   176	        case IDENTIFIER -> {
   177	          next();
   178	          switch (lookahead) {
   179	            case COLON, ASSIGN, LBRACE -> {
   180	              backtrack();

    14	  private FullToken next() {
    15	    if (backtracking) {
    16	      backtracking = false;
    17	      lookahead = _lookahead.token;
    18	      spanLookahead = _lookahead.span;
    19	      return prev;
    20	    }
    21	    prev = _lookahead;
    22	    _lookahead = forceNext();
    23	    lookahead = _lookahead.token;
    24	    spanLookahead = _lookahead.span;
    25	    return prev;
    26	  }
    27	
    28	  private FullToken forceNext() {
    29	    var tk = lexer.next();
    30	    precededBySemicolon = false;
    31	    while (tk == Token.LINE_COMMENT
    32	        || tk == Token.BLOCK_COMMENT
    33	        || tk == Token.SEMICOLON
    34	        || tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
    35	      precededBySemicolon = precededBySemicolon || tk == Token.SEMICOLON;
    36	      tk = lexer.next();
    37	    }
    38	    return new FullToken(tk, lexer.span(), lexer.newLinesBetween);
    39	  }
    40	
    41	  // Like next, but don't ignore comments
    42	  private FullToken nextComment() {
    43	    prev = _lookahead;
    44	    _lookahead = forceNextComment();
    45	    lookahead = _lookahead.token;
    46	    spanLookahead = _lookahead.span;
    47	    return prev;
    48	  }

public class ReproShebang {

    18	import java.util.ArrayDeque;
    19	import java.util.Deque;
    20	import org.pkl.parser.util.ErrorMessages;
    21	
    22	public class Lexer {
    23	
    24	  private final char[] source;
    25	  private final int size;
    26	  protected int cursor = 0;
    27	  protected int sCursor = 0;
    28	  private char lookahead;
    29	  private State state = State.DEFAULT;
    30	  private final Deque<InterpolationScope> interpolationStack = new ArrayDeque<>();
    31	  private boolean stringEnded = false;
    32	  private boolean isEscape = false;
    33	  // how many newlines exist between two subsequent tokens
    34	  protected int newLinesBetween = 0;
    35	
    36	  private static final char EOF = Short.MAX_VALUE;
    37	
    38	  public Lexer(String input) {
    39	    source = input.toCharArray();
    40	    size = source.length;
    41	    if (size > 0) {
    42	      lookahead = source[cursor];
    43	    } else {
    44	      lookahead = EOF;
    45	    }
    46	  }
    47	
    48	  // The span of the last lexed token
    49	  public Span span() {
    50	    return new Span(sCursor, cursor - sCursor);
    51	  }
    52	
    53	  // The text of the last lexed token
    54	  public String text() {
    55	    return new String(source, sCursor, cursor - sCursor);
    56	  }
    57	
    58	  public char[] getSource() {
    59	    return source;
    60	  }
    61	
    62	  public String textFor(int offset, int size) {
    63	    return new String(source, offset, size);
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  public Token next() {
    67	    sCursor = cursor;
    68	    newLinesBetween = 0;
    69	    return switch (state) {
    70	      case DEFAULT -> nextDefault();
    71	      case STRING -> nextString();
    72	    };
    73	  }
    74	
    75	  private Token nextDefault() {
    76	    var ch = nextChar();
    77	    // ignore spaces
    78	    while (ch == ' ' || ch == '\n' || ch == '\t' || ch == '\f' || ch == '\r') {
    79	      sCursor = cursor;
    80	      if (ch == '\n') {
    81	        newLinesBetween++;
    82	      }
    83	      ch = nextChar();
    84	    }
    85	    return switch (ch) {
    86	      case EOF -> {
    87	        // when EOF is reached we overshot the span
    88	        cursor--;
    89	        yield Token.EOF;
    90	      }
    91	      case ';' -> Token.SEMICOLON;
    92	      case '(' -> {
    93	        var scope = interpolationStack.peek();
    94	        if (scope != null) {
    95	          scope.parens++;
    96	        }
    97	        yield Token.LPAREN;
    98	      }
    99	      case ')' -> {
   100	        var scope = interpolationStack.peek();
   101	        if (scope != null) {
   102	          scope.parens--;
   103	          if (scope.parens <= 0) {
   104	            // interpolation is over. Back to string
   105	            state = State.STRING;
   106	          }
   107	        }
   108	        yield Token.RPAREN;
   109	      }
   110	      case '{' -> Token.LBRACE;
   111	      case '}' -> Token.RBRACE;
   112	      case ',' -> Token.COMMA;
   113	      case '@' -> Token.AT;
   114	      case ':' -> Token.COLON;
   115	      case '+' -> Token.PLUS;
   116	      case '%' -> Token.MOD;
   117	      case '[' -> {
   118	        if (lookahead == '[') {
   119	          nextChar();
   120	          yield Token.LPRED;

    28	      return Token.FLOAT;
    29	    }
    30	    return Token.INT;
    31	  }
    32	
    33	  private Token lexSlash() {
    34	    switch (lookahead) {
    35	      case '/':
    36	        {
    37	          nextChar();
    38	          var token = lookahead == '/' ? Token.DOC_COMMENT : Token.LINE_COMMENT;
    39	          while (lookahead != '\n' && lookahead != '\r' && lookahead != EOF) {
    40	            nextChar();
    41	          }
    42	          return token;
    43	        }
    44	      case '*':
    45	        {
    46	          nextChar();
    47	          lexBlockComment();
    48	          return Token.BLOCK_COMMENT;
    49	        }
    50	      default:
    51	        return Token.DIV;
    52	    }
    53	  }
    54	
    55	  private void lexBlockComment() {
    56	    if (lookahead == EOF) throw unexpectedEndOfFile();
    57	    var prev = nextChar();
    58	    while (lookahead != EOF) {
    59	      if (prev == '*' && lookahead == '/') {
    60	        nextChar();
    61	        break;
    62	      }
    63	      prev = nextChar();
    64	    }
    65	    if (lookahead == EOF) throw unexpectedEndOfFile();
    66	  }
    67	
    68	  private void lexHexNumber() {
    69	    if (lookahead == '_') {
    70	      throw lexError("invalidSeparatorPosition");
    71	    }
    72	    if (!isHex(lookahead)) {
    73	      throw unexpectedChar(lookahead, "hexadecimal number");
    74	    }
    75	    while (isHex(lookahead) || lookahead == '_') {
    76	      nextChar();
    77	    }
    78	  }
    79	
    80	  private void lexBinNumber() {
    81	    if (lookahead == '_') {
    82	      throw lexError("invalidSeparatorPosition");
    83	    }
    84	    if (!(lookahead == '0' || lookahead == '1')) {
    85	      throw unexpectedChar(lookahead, "binary number");
    86	    }
    87	    while (lookahead == '0' || lookahead == '1' || lookahead == '_') {
    88	      nextChar();
    89	    }
    90	  }
    91

diff --git a/repro_shebang.py b/repro_shebang.py
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..025f94fc

@@ -0,0 +1,50 @@
+import subprocess, textwrap, os, sys, tempfile, pathlib
+
+SRC_OK = """#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval
+
+foo = 1
+"""
+SRC_BAD = """foo = 1
+
+#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval
+"""
+
+JAVA = r'''
+import org.pkl.parser.Parser;
+
+public class ReproShebang {
+  public static void main(String[] args) {
+    String src = args[0].equals("ok") ? """%s""" : """%s""";
+    Parser p = new Parser();
+    try {
+      p.parseModule(src);
+      System.out.println("PARSED");
+    } catch (Exception e) {
+      System.out.println("ERROR: " + e.getClass().getName());
+      System.out.println(e.getMessage());
+      System.exit(2);
+    }
+  }
+}
+''' % (SRC_OK.replace('\\','\\\\').replace('"""','\\"\\"\\"'), SRC_BAD.replace('\\','\\\\').replace('"""','\\"\\"\\"'))
+
+root = pathlib.Path(__file__).resolve().parent
+build = root/".repro_build"
+build.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
+(java_file:=build/"ReproShebang.java").write_text(JAVA)
+
+# build parser jar/classes
+subprocess.check_call(['./gradlew','-q',':pkl-parser:classes'])
+
+# compile repro
+cp = str(root/'pkl-parser/build/classes/java/main')
+subprocess.check_call(['javac','-cp',cp,'-d',str(build),str(java_file)])
+
+# run ok and bad
+for mode in ("ok","bad"):
+    print('==',mode,'==')
+    r = subprocess.run(['java','-cp',f"{build}:{cp}", 'ReproShebang', mode], text=True, capture_output=True)
+    print(r.stdout)
+    if r.returncode not in (0,2):
+        print(r.stderr)
+        sys.exit(r.returncode)

@@ -0,0 +1,35 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env bash
+set -euo pipefail
+
+./gradlew -q :pkl-parser:classes
+
+cat > /tmp/ReproShebang.java <<'JAVA'
+import org.pkl.parser.Parser;
+
+public class ReproShebang {
+  static final String SRC_OK = "#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\n\nfoo = 1\n";
+  static final String SRC_BAD = "foo = 1\n\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\n";
+
+  public static void main(String[] args) {
+    String src = args.length > 0 && args[0].equals("ok") ? SRC_OK : SRC_BAD;
+    Parser p = new Parser();
+    try {
+      p.parseModule(src);
+      System.out.println("PARSED");
+    } catch (Exception e) {
+      System.out.println("ERROR: " + e.getClass().getName());
+      System.out.println(e.getMessage());
+      System.exit(2);
+    }
+  }
+}
+JAVA
+
+javac -cp pkl-parser/build/classes/java/main -d /tmp /tmp/ReproShebang.java
+
+echo "== ok =="
+java -cp /tmp:pkl-parser/build/classes/java/main ReproShebang ok
+
+echo "== bad =="
+set +e
+java -cp /tmp:pkl-parser/build/classes/java/main ReproShebang bad
